The ADE - Purchase, Commitment, Stock and Intake semantic model has a health score of 0/100 (Grade F). It contains 81 tables (23 DirectQuery, 46 Dual), 235 measures, and 230 relationships (4 bidirectional). BPA detected 1258 findings (9 high, 14 medium). DAX analysis found 3 FILTER(ALL) anti-patterns and 2 measures generating 5+ SQL subqueries.

Key Findings & Recommended Actions (6 total — 0 critical, 2 high)

F1
high
4 Bidirectional Cross-Filter Relationships
Change to single-direction unless explicitly required. Use CROSSFILTER() in specific measures if needed.
Semantic Model 30-50% reduction in SQL queries for affected visuals.
F6
high
10 Pass-Through Serve Views (>50 cols, no filter)
Create narrow serve views selecting only columns used by PBI measures.
Engineering 60-70% reduction in read_bytes for affected tables.

See section Detailed Recommendations for full implementation guides.

4. Best Practice Findings

Rule Violations

RuleViolationsImpact TypePerformance Impact
AVOID_BIDIRECTIONAL_RELATIONSHIPS 4 Latency Generates additional SQL round-trips for bidirectional filter propagation. Can double the number of queries per visual.
DUAL_MODE_TABLES 5 Latency May trigger unnecessary DirectQuery when Import would suffice. Dual tables are processed twice during refresh.
FILTER_ALL_ANTIPATTERN 3 Latency Forces full table scan in DirectQuery mode. Each FILTER(ALL) adds an unfiltered subquery to the generated SQL.
WIDE_TABLES 9 Cost More columns increases bytes read per query. Primarily a cost issue; latency impact depends on whether I/O is the bottleneck.
MISSING_FORMAT_STRING 2 Quality No performance impact. Missing format strings affect display consistency and user experience.
BARE_DIVISION 1 Quality Risk of division-by-zero errors. No direct performance impact, but errors can cause visual rendering failures.
DAX_COLUMNS_NOT_FULLY_QUALIFIED 44 Quality Readability and maintenance issue. No performance impact but increases risk of errors when columns are renamed.
UNUSED_COLUMNS_CANDIDATE 1190 Cost Hidden/unused columns are still included in DirectQuery SQL. Increases read bytes and cost per query.

✓ 4 of 12 rules passed (no violations): AVOID_FLOATING_POINT_DATA_TYPES, AVOID_IFERROR, MANY_TO_MANY_RELATIONSHIPS, AUTO_DATE_TABLES

7. Recommendation Quadrant

Quick Wins (Low Effort, High Impact)

    Strategic Investments (Higher Effort, High Impact)

    • F2: 3 FILTER(ALL) Anti-Patterns Semantic Model

    8. Detailed Recommendations

    Implementation details, trade-offs, and alternative options for each finding.

    F1: 4 Bidirectional Cross-Filter Relationships

    high Model-wide Semantic Model

    Problem: 4 relationships use bidirectional cross-filtering. In DirectQuery mode, each can double the number of SQL queries per visual.

    How to Fix

    Change to single-direction unless explicitly required. Use CROSSFILTER() in specific measures if needed.

    Estimated improvement: 30-50% reduction in SQL queries for affected visuals.

    Impact: medium Effort: low
    Trade-offs:
    • May break visuals relying on cross-filter direction

    F2: 3 FILTER(ALL) Anti-Patterns

    medium Model-wide Semantic Model

    Problem: 3 DAX measures use FILTER(ALL()) which forces full table scans in DirectQuery. Combined with large fact tables, each generates an unfiltered subquery.

    How to Fix

    Refactor to REMOVEFILTERS() or direct CALCULATE predicates. Prioritise measures on high-traffic pages.

    Estimated improvement: 20-40% latency reduction per refactored measure.

    Impact: medium Effort: high
    Requires Deep Dive
    1. Run top 10 FILTER(ALL) measures in DAX Studio with Server Timings
    2. Compare SE vs FE time split
    Trade-offs:
    • Requires thorough testing for calculation equivalence

    F3: 9 Wide Tables (>50 columns)

    medium Model-wide Semantic Model Engineering

    Problem: 9 tables have >50 columns. In DirectQuery, all columns are included in generated SQL.

    How to Fix

    Audit unused columns and remove from model. Consider narrow serve views.

    Estimated improvement: Proportional reduction in read_bytes per query.

    Impact: medium Effort: medium
    Trade-offs:
    • Column removal requires coordination with report authors

    F4: 1190 Unused Column Candidates

    medium Model-wide Semantic Model

    Problem: 1190 columns not referenced in any DAX measure. Candidates for removal to reduce DQ payload.

    How to Fix

    Audit columns, verify not used in visuals/slicers, remove confirmed unused.

    Estimated improvement: Cost reduction — fewer bytes read per query.

    Impact: low Effort: medium
    Trade-offs:
    • Some may be used in visuals or bookmarks

    F5: 5 Dual-Mode Tables Could Be Import

    medium Model-wide Semantic Model

    Problem: 5 tables in Dual mode are hidden or have no relationships. Switch to Import to reduce DQ overhead.

    How to Fix

    Switch to Import mode in Tabular Editor.

    Estimated improvement: Minor — reduces refresh time and DQ calls.

    Impact: low Effort: low
    Trade-offs:
    • Verify no visual references these in DQ mode

    F6: 10 Pass-Through Serve Views (>50 cols, no filter)

    high Model-wide Engineering

    Problem: 10 dbt serve views are SELECT * pass-throughs with >50 columns and no WHERE filter.

    How to Fix

    Create narrow serve views selecting only columns used by PBI measures.

    Estimated improvement: 60-70% reduction in read_bytes for affected tables.

    Impact: high Effort: low
    Trade-offs:
    • Must audit PBI column usage before narrowing
